{"kind": "blogger#postList", "nextPageToken": "CgkIChig4sGA0yUQy4Ca9ZL8nrwx", "items": [{"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "6248612764525248517", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2011-01-03T13:30:00+05:30", "updated": "2011-01-03T13:30:18+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMjk0MDQxNjE4NTk3Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/01/ar-afff-on-chemical-tankers-capt-ajit.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/6248612764525248517", "title": "AR-AFFF ON CHEMICAL TANKERS --  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSF_iuE47kI/AAAAAAAACkA/pzfKNqb9J3c/s1600/s.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSF_iuE47kI/AAAAAAAACkA/pzfKNqb9J3c/s1600/s.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSF_oo2jlwI/AAAAAAAACkE/fNyTdrrSm2s/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSF_oo2jlwI/AAAAAAAACkE/fNyTdrrSm2s/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSF_szKVpHI/AAAAAAAACkI/WL8TKDpWvao/s1600/chm.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TSF_szKVpHI/AAAAAAAACkI/WL8TKDpWvao/s1600/chm.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">AR-AFFF &nbsp;- &nbsp;</span></b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Alcohol Resistant<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Aqueous Film Forming Foam concentrate ( free flowing ).<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><o:p>Four stripers who go to shipyards to take delivery of brand new chemical tankers, must be familiar with the following. &nbsp;I had once joined a 12 year old stainless chemical tanker with animal protein foam inside the foam tanks, and i had to twist my company's arm ( packed with pretenders ) &nbsp;by threatening to hold up the ship , &nbsp;before they would spend budget money and change the foam concentrate. &nbsp;</o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><o:p>Remember this is NOT about certification or inspectors or audits -- it is about lives at sea, you have sworn to protect.</o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">The rate of foam supply on a chemical tanker is 3 times more than that of a usual annex 1 tanker. &nbsp;Portable foam is also required ( in addition to fixed ) for small isolated fires.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">Regular protein foam should not be used on chemical tankers. For cargoes for which foam is NOT compatible, dry powder or water spray can be used. Take this information from column \u201c l \u201c of the IBC code table for min requirements.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><b><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; mso-ansi-language: EN;\">AR-AFFF</span></b><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; mso-ansi-language: EN;\"> is a synthetic foam developed for BOTH hydrocarbon and polar solvent&nbsp;materials. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Polar solvents are combustible liquids that destroy conventional fire fighting foam. These solvents extract the water contained in the foam, breaking down the foam blanket. Therefore, these fuels require an alcohol or polar solvent resistant foam. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Alcohol resistant foam must be bounced off of a surface and allowed to flow down and over the liquid to form its membrane, compared to standard AFFF that can be sprayed directly onto the fire. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">AR-AFFF is intended for use at a 6% proportioning rate means 6 parts AR-AFFF concentrate to 94 parts water. It can be used on polar solvent/water miscible fuels such as alcohols, ketones, esters, etc. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>It is suitable for use with either fresh or salt water<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span class=\"A3\"><span style=\"color: windowtext; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;\">First, an aqueous film is formed in the case of a conventional hydrocarbon fuel, or a polymeric membrane in the case of a polar solvent fuel. This film or membrane forms a barrier to help prevent the release of fuel vapor<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span class=\"A3\"><span style=\"color: windowtext; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;\">Second, regardless of the fuel type, a foam blanket is formed which excludes oxygen and from which drains the liquids that form the film or the polymeric membrane.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span class=\"A3\"><span style=\"color: windowtext; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%; mso-ansi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;\">Third, the water content of the foam produces a cooling effect.</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"> When used on polar solvent liquids (such as alcohols, ketones and esters) a tough, polymeric membrane layer is formed to separate the foam blanket from the polar fuel, and help prevent vapor emissions. ) with the addition of a synthesized polymer. Such polymers allow the foam to form a layer that encases it from the fuel.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">As a result, AR-AFFF compounds can be applied to fires where the fuel is miscible with water (e.g., alcohols). function is to make the foam more stable and heat resistant, resulting in better burnback resistance and sealability compared to conventional AFFF<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Alcohol resistant foams should be used in fighting fires of fuels containing oxygenates, eg. MTBE&nbsp;or fires of liquids based on or containing polar&nbsp;solvents .</span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"> </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">Foam concentrates for use on polar solvents differ from standard AFFFs because they contain hydrophilic polymer which enable these products to effectively extinguish polar solvent fires when proportioned at their designed percentages, either at 3% or 6%. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">The hydrated hydrophilic polymer coagulates and comes out of solution when the foam contacts the water soluble polar solvent, forming a cohesive polymeric layer on the fuel surface. This polymeric layer prevents the polar solvent from attacking the foam. The presence of the polymer in AR-AFFF makes the concentrate look different than a standard AFFF; <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">AR-AFFF is thicker and also appears more opaque than AFFF</span>. &nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">Despite its increased apparent viscosity, AR-AFFF is sheer thinning, non-newtonian fluid which will proportion effectively through equipment designed to proportion standard AFFFs.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">Care must be taken when storing AR-AFFF to ensure that polymer remain fluid and do not gel in the storage tank or piping. The following precaution must be taken to prevent gelling problems :<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">Since the product is designed to gel when come in contact with a polar solvent, polar solvents introduced in storage will cause gelling. This includes ethylene glycol which is sometimes used to reduce the freezing point of products</span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">. Ethylene glycol or any other polar solvent must not be added to the foam concentrate in storage.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">Other foam liquid concentrates should not be mixed with AR-AFFF in storage. This includes AFFFs, other brands of alcohol resistant concentrates, fluoroprotein and protein foams.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">Different types of foam concentrates should never be mixed since they may be incompatible and all manufacturer warranties would be voided since long-term performance of a given agent could not be validated.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">This is recognized by NFPA 11 - Low Expansion Foam Combined Agent Systems, \u201cDifferent types and brands of concentrates might be incompatible and shall not be mixed in storage.\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">AR-AFFF is sensitive to high concentrations of metal ions in solution. Excess metal ions can come from a carbon steel tank or piping particularly when a large surface area of carbon steel is in contact with a small amount of AR-AFFF. This is usually the case in small diameter pipe. A large carbon steel tank filled with AR-AFFF has a relatively small amount of surface contact area compared to the mass of AR-AFFF, Carbon steel is not the most suitable material of construction for an AR-AFFF storage tank. The most common recommended materials of construction in use today for AR-AFFF are : the original container, carbon steel with an approved coating, stainless steel, approved plastic or fiberglass, or a bladder tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">Another situation to avoid is the use of dissimilar metals in an AR-AFFF foam storage system. Dissimilar metals such as a stainless steel tank and a brass valve will cause galvanic corrosion and will increase the metal ion content in the AR-AFFF concentrate which can cause gelling. Dissimilar metals should either not be used in the concentrate system or they should be isolated by a non-conductive gasketing material. By avoiding or isolating dissimilar metals, the tank and piping will last longer as galvanic corrosion is prevented.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">If AR-AFFF concentrate is allowed to evaporate freely, the water and solvent in the concentrate will evaporate causing a skin of polymer to form on the surface of the concentrate. The skin could plug the proportioning orifices. To eliminate this possibility, the concentrate tank must be sealed to prevent evaporation and a vacuum breaker installed to break the seal when the system is in use.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">Evaporation losses will also be minimized by keeping the concentrate tanks full. If it is not possible to seal the tank, a thin layer of mineral oil can be applied to the surface of the concentrate to reduce evaporation.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">The concentrate should be stored within its usable temperature range which is 20- 49C) for non-freeze protected concentrates. Freeze protected concentrates should stored at temperature specified/designated by their manufacturer. If the product freezes, it can be thawed and agitated before using.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">Container should not be exposed to direct heat and light.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">METHODOLOGY OF ADDITION OF OIL OVER THE SURFACE OF FOAM CONCENTRATE (ALCOHOL TYPE) WHEN STORED IN STORAGE TANKS<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">The quantity of oil required should be calculated as per the size and area of the tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">The thickness of oil layer over the foam concentrate should be minimum 4 - 6 mm.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">By using a funnel and a pipe, oil should be gently poured over the surface of the foam concentrate.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">The one end of the pipe will be attached to the funnel and other end of the pipe should be just above the surface of the foam concentrate while pouring the oil.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">The oil should be added at different points of the tank, so that the oil is uniformly spread over the surface of the foam concentrate.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">If there is a single opening or a small opening, then add half the quantity of oil over the surface of the foam concentrate gently. Wait till the oil spreads over the foam concentrate and then add the balance quantity of oil so that the complete area is covered by oil with a minimum thickness of 4 - 6mm.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">The discharge of the foam concentrate when stored in a tank should be from the bottom of the tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">The foam in the tank should not be completely utilized as there are chances of oil entering into the fire fighting system.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">The foam should not be added over the surface of the oil.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">Foam concentrate should be poured by using a funnel and a pipe.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">For any reason, if you cannot use a funnel and a pipe, the foam concentrate can be put directly over the surface of the oil<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">Even if foam falls over the surface of the oil, it will not affect the quality of the foam because:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">As the density of foam is higher than the density of oil, it will settle down and the oil will float over the surface. Oil is immiscible in foam.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;
