margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Master should forward a copy of his proposed stow to the chemical operator with&nbsp; info--</span></i><u1:p></u1:p><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Cargo density at 20<sup>o</sup>C<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Correction factor per<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><sup>o</sup>/centigrade<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Carriage temperature (if any) Min/ Max carriage temperatures(if any)<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">If Nitrogen is required either to inert the tank(s) before loading or to maintain a blanket during the voyage, then on board Nitrogen stock and intake capacity should be checked and arrangements made to supply any additional requirements.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Draeger tubes should be checked and if necessary ordered- especially if the VP/ TLV ratio is high.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">USCG Group.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Marpol category; XYZ or Annex I. (Certain ports like Rotterdam have their own Marpol categories).<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The following steps should be carried out ( just a few major items ) :-</span></i><u1:p></u1:p><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></i></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Identify the cargo should be identified using the US Coast Guard book.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The relevant MSDS sheet must be read in detail.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Recheck the density and correction factors .<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">For PRE calculations, the maximum quantity and the maximum anticipated temperatures should be used not the loading temperatures . Any lesser quantities/temperatures will of course require less cubic capacity.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Coating compatibility for the product required to be carried to be checked.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Adjacent bulkheads should be checked for product compatibility.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The required volumetric capacity should be checked against the available capacity in the nominated tanks.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Loading restrictions i.e. deck tank weight loading, high density loading and tank filling limits etc.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Checked for any special requirements, i.e. nitrogen, heating, non-heating, inhibited,<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Antidotes required should be checked and replenished if necessary.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Draeger tubes for the product--if applicable. The Drager list should be checked for expiry dates and tubes ordered as required<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">FOSFA banned list, NIOP banned list.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Back loading should be anticipated. For example. If a cargo is discharged and is being prepared for the next cargo before adjacent tanks are to be discharged, can hot water and/or steam be used for cleaning?<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB;\">Company policy requires that no tank is loaded to a volume of greater than 98% at any time. For cargoes like wine, take the permission of the chemical operator.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><b><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Letter of Protest:</span><u1:p></u1:p></i></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Present Letters of Protest to terminal personnel for following, if applicable:</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Slow Loading Rate</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Free Water In Cargo</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Ship / Shore Figures Discrepancy</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Flow Rate Restrictions</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Loading / Discharging Connections</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Manifold Pressure Restrictions</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Delay Due High Back Pressure</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">ROB After Discharge</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Refusal To Sign Vessel\u2019s Cargo Documents</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">General LOP for any other condition you feel is protecting the owner\u2019s interests. eg. terminal delays, unsafe berth, etc.</span></i><u1:p></u1:p><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">If the vessel is encountering a very high back pressure and is only using a small percentage of her pumping power available, a protest should be issued.&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>A discharge can take several days because of excessive back pressure and the ship may only be able to run cargo pumps at reduced speed<o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">If in your opinion, the ship tanks are rejected at load port in an unfair manner immediately advise the chemical operator by mobile phone who will take immediate steps to give you assistance in cleaning or rectifying the situation. You should if unable to make the phone contact , place the parties concerned on written notice<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">If terminal does not give the labour to connect hoses, issue a letter of protest before telling ships crew to do so.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">During discharge if manifold pressure drops ,increase the pump speed or put more pumps in line.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Protest for discharge restrictions to ship and shore delays must be issued without fail<o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Proposed load should be entered into the ship\u2019s loadicator for stresses. Any draft restrictions&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>seasonal loadlines etc. should also be checked. Also check load/ discharge sequence&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>to avoid list/trim/draft/stress problems and loss of berth time.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Bear in mind--actual density and temperatures may not be supplied until<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span><b><i>after</i></b><span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>loading has commenced.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The use of flexible hoses must be minimized, with fixed U/Y pieces used wherever possible. The cargo hose test certificates should be available for perusal.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The handling procedures including the maximum loading or unloading rates must be agreed in writing. Complete and sign the appropriate safety check list, showing the main safety precautions to be taken before and during such operations and also the action to be taken in the event of an emergency .<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The Master has a responsibility to check that the terminal has also made proper preparations for the safe operation .<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The number of valves to be closed during the topping off period should be reduced to a minimum. Always give the shore min 10 minutes warning of completion of loading.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Chief Officer should be identify the type of pump(s) being used for loading at the pre load&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>conference and understand and agree emergency shutdown procedures.&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>Topping up by gravity is the best , or even a centrifugal pump .&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>A positive displacement pump like reciprocating or screw pump will continue to build up&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>pressure until the hose bursts.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">When connecting flanges, bolts should be cross tightened, to ensure that the flange faces are mated properly.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">All connections must be pressure tested to check for any leakages. Leaks can be detected by pressurising the connection with either air or nitrogen and then brushing soapy water around the gasket. The connections must be de-pressurised before adjustments are made to the connections.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The pre-loading meeting should include the following written&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>information:--<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The sequence of transfer operations.</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The agreed loading/discharge rate. These rates must not exceed the vessel\u2019s capabilities at any time and loading rates must take into account that the vessel may load through her cargo pumps,</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Details of the shore the lines to be used.</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Critical stages, ie Topping off rate.</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Standby time for topping off</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Shore tank changes</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Line blowing</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Local terminal/port authority regulations ( say fire wire height )</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Emergency procedures</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Containment procedures</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Reporting procedures</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Shut down procedures</span></i><u1:p></u1:p><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The cargo discharge / load plan must be signed by all deck crew.The manifold rigging plan and the bar diagram must be made .The ship shore safety checklists, preloading/ discharge, during, after checklists must be familiarized. In USA the cargo transfer procedures must be posted in the approved format. Pre-loading cargo calculations must take into account the shore tank temperatures , so that the SG of cargo at observed temperatures can be calculated.&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>Take into account if the surveyors calculations are based on ASTM method or by the density correction based on temperature difference.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB;\">Ullages, temperatures and water dips of all cargo tanks are to be taken jointly by ship and shore personnel, using closed sampling and gauging equipment and the net quantity of cargo on board calculated:</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">on completion of loading</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">before commencing discharge</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">on completion of discharge if same bottom cargo remains on board</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">prior to loading if same bottom cargo is already on board from a previous port</span><u1:p></u1:p></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">prior to and immediately after any transfer of cargo</span></i><u1:p></u1:p><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB;\">The net quantity of cargo on board is to be agreed between the ship and terminal representatives:</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">before disconnecting the last cargo hose on completion of loading<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">before commencing any cargo discharge<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The Chief officer must personally cross check that the ship\u2019s cargo system has been configured properly for the cargo and all plugs and drains have been re-positioned.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN;\">A usual problem is lack of clear instructions and information being given to Duty Officers who will be involved with cargo operations. Many chief officers try to keep total control and monopoly of the cargo and ballast operations and the Duty Officer learns very little about cargo and port procedures. And then while appraising the junior officer at the end of his contract he is termed as&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>\u201c useless\u2014not to be re-employed \u201d which is not true.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN;\">As we have bridge team management, the same way we must have cargo team management. Chief officers should delegate the duties in a proper manner to the duty officers whilst still maintaining overall control. This will allow the junior officers to gain knowledge and confidence and prevent the chief officer from getting fatigued.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB;\">All Deck Officers and the Pumpman shall commit to memory the arrangements of all cargo , ballast and other piping systems , so that they may deal immediately with any emergency situation .</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">All valves in the cargo piping systems and ballast systems shall be CLOSED at all times except when they are required to be OPEN for operational reasons.&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>Valves, which are OPEN, shall be CLOSED as soon as operational requirements permit<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Manifold valves must not be OPENED until hoses are connected and must be CLOSED before hoses are disconnected.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Remote valves which cannot be lashed to maintain its status quo shall be temporarily labelled&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>\"DO NOT OPERATE\"<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN;\">No loading / discharging can be done without pre-planning by mans of a bar diagram.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Tank entry tagging system must be there on all ships. HHR board must be filled.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The OOW must be given additionally a load/ dischg plan plus a bar diagram for cargo/ ballast operations.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Before the Chief officer leaves the CCR/ deck for resting he must give clear written instructions in a dedicated cargo order book&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>to the OOD regarding the continuance of current operations and the time or circumstances when he is to be called. The OOW must be given additionally a load/ dischg plan plus a bar diagram for cargo/ ballast operations.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB;\">The OOD shall not depart from the plan without direct instructions from the Chief officer. He shall call him immediately if any emergency arises or any unforeseen circumstance arises.&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>In an emergency he shall not hesitate to stop all operations if he considers that the circumstances deem such a drastic action.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB;\">The OOD shall record the events of the operations as they occur in the LAN electronic log and the cargo log book. Electronic port log fed into the CCR computer is connected by LAN to other ships computers . The cargo loaded/ discharged plus the balance to go plus the ETC must be mentioned every 6 hours.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB;\">Manifold drip trays should be regularly cleaned and dried after each cargo operation to remove any spillage which may be incompatible with another chemical&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>spilled later.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB;\">Deck booster pumps are used when discharging homogeneous cargoes, to increase the bulk discharge rate or when discharging viscous cargoes such as molasses. Screw pumps must not be started with the delivery valve shut.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The amount of cargo to be loaded and the type quantity i.e. [ moloo/ molco/ min-max].<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;In the event of a min/ max cargo, the vessel should endeavor to arrange a shore stop for the product and note it down in the SOF. In other cases, the vessel should endeavor to lift the maximum cargo possible within the percentage options.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Where the ships tanks have to precleaned immediately after dischg the cleaning gear must be rigged before tank dry certificate is issued.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The chemical operator must be advised of any pipeline leaks or bulkhead structure cargo leaks. The condition of tanks including discolouration, residue , scale , sediment must be advised.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">TCFW monitoring is Chief officers sole responsibility. Running out of water when ship is outside for tankcleaning in not acceptable. Of for the matter getting a TCFW tank contaminated with salt water. Tank cleaning preparation must include a bar diagram. If cargoes have to be heated steam and fuel requirement must be discussed with Chief engineer.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Do not use the vacuum side of PV valve in auto mode for discharging.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Remote gauging system should be calibrated by means of comparison with reference MMC tape after every loading and before every discharge.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">New chemicals evolve almost daily . Ship should be aware of relevant cargo specs , handling procedures and tank cleaning procedures. All doubts must be addressed with the company chemical operator.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">If possible load cargoes which require nitrogen blanketing first\u2014so that time is not wasted.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Chemical must be named in all documents exactly as it is described in the bill of lading<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">In different berths with different&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>consignees, the new NOR will be when the hoses get disconnected.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">In case the agents are authorized to sign the bill of lading\u2014and the figures are unknown\u2014<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The final B/L figures should be emailed to the master for his scrutiny and agreement before the B/Ls\u2019 are released.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Request from ship for reducing rates for topping off are not to be mentioned in the SOF but any shore reduction must be mentioned.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">To prevent overloading/ underloading the dock water density must be taken before commencement of loading and just before completion<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">In case of pigging the pigging in quantity must be declared by shore in advance to prevent overflow of last tank<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Pumping logs must be endorsed by the loading master or the terminal rep.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Manifold valve must always be opened last. Even if there is a stop of transfer for a few minutes\u2014the manifold valve must always be shut.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Stopping transfer:<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Cargo flow while loading must be stopped by shore valves and vice versa while discharging.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Avoid using common collector while handling high MP cargoes like Phenol which may freeze. Otherwise use it every time possible\u2014unless the cargo is incompatible with the ships cargo hose.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Always take off unused spool pieces and blank them \u2014on chemical tankers 2 or 3 valve segregation is not considered effective.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">After connection test the spools with 4 kg air and soap solution. After air test make sure the pressure is released. Also the SS nuts and bolts can loosen up after a long voyage due to low friction factor\u2014it is not advisable to grease the butterworth port bolt threads as vibration caused slack nuts/ bolts can cause sea water ingress on ships having low freeboard.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Maintain valve open board in CCR and also a valve reference strip on valve wheel ( a mark which shows if a valve is shut or open ). This is the only way the duty officer\u2019s rounds on deck of a manual tanker with dozens of valves on deck can be termed meaningful. He should be able to see which all valves or drain cocks are open without handling them physically.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Check manifold connection at low initial flow rate\u2014 Caution: for solidifying cargoes\u2014do NOT do this low initial rate check, lest the cargo freezes inside.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Do NOT air blow while discharging into submarine terminals--unless you want the submerged hose to rip asunder and your company to come down.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">If tank lines and drains have to be opened to be proved dry then the certificate must be endorsed to show this fact.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">During the voyage internal transfer of cargo must NEVER be done without charterers approval, unless in imminent and dire emergency. The checklists must be filled up and the ORB must be entered.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Residues from manifold drip trays must be transferred into slop tank , drain tank or retaining container. First ensure that the contents are compatible.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Care should be taken to ensure that cargo vapour does not enter the engine .&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>Internal combustion engines can over speed and destroy themselves if flammable vapour is present in the air supply, even at concentration well below LFL.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">The use of mobile phones and radio pagers is prohibited except within the ships accommodation.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">For visitors: Mobile phones and radio pagers should be switched off at gangway and only switched on when inside the ships accommodation.<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>A warning notice to this effect should be posted at ships gangway.<o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">If at any time at sea or in port an oil slick on the sea is sighted in the vicinity of the ship it shall be reported to the Master who shall ensure that the oil slick is not being caused by his ship. The Master shall also record the sighting in the Deck Log Book stating that the oil was not discharged by his ship.The Company shall be advised of this sighting in writing if the slick is major.<o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ansi-language: EN-GB;\">At least one copy of each cargo related document, which is signed by ship's personnel, is to be retained on board in the ship's files.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">During loading operations, access to the accommodation is to be restricted to one entry point only and this should be agreed prior to the vessel\u2019s arrival at the load port. All other doors and ports should remain closed throughout the loading operation.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">To assist accurate assessment of the wind direction, a flag ( or a wind sock ) to be placed on deck in vicinity of the vapour emissions during venting, it should to be illuminated at night. This is not applicable for ships having a repeater of anemometer in CCR.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">There shall be no work aloft POISONOUS LOAD PASSAGE carried out other than that directly related to the operational safety or navigation of the vessel and if carried out to be under the control of a hazardous task permit. Recharging of BA cylinders during loading is not to be carried out unless air quality at the compressor inlet vicinity is continuously monitored.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; vertical-align: baseline;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Prior to arrival at the discharge port the vessel must&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>reduce the cargo tank pressure to the lowest acceptable level in order to reduce the possibility of having to vent tanks whilst at the berth.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Times of High and Low waters must be posted at gangway.&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>Also minimum depth of water at berth and maximum draught permitted.&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>Gangway and Deck Watch must be aware of tide times.<o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Master should ensure that the mooring configuration suits his own vessel and get it rectified after consulting the pilot, especially if the chemical hose connections are rigid chiksan types. Most chemical tankers berth at river ports where there is strong current and tide range.&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>The tidal information must be available in CCR too.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">If the quay fenders do not abut against the vertical shell of the vessel, the ship should be repositioned and the MOT gangway used in a safe manner. Most parcel chemical tankers have ductile steel hull with vertical corrugations of athwarthship bulkheads.&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>If there is danger of ship is main deck&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>going below the quay level, it will be necessary to completely reposition the MOT gangway for this period, under personal supervision of OOW and a proper gangway watch maintained for safe access.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">When there is strong current and rigid chiksan at manifold, springs must be adjusted only under personal supervision of OOW. It must be remembered that it is not possible to pull the ship against the affects of current and wind. Commonsense dictates that springs which are slack must be tightened.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Main engines must not be tried out with air and fuel at berth, unless the OOW personally checks that the springs are taut and the gangway will not get damaged or become unsafe due to ship\u2019s surge. During this period gangway throughfare must be prohibited, especially if the chemical cargo is harmful for humans and the environment.&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>As far as possible MOT gangway must be rigged aft of manifold, as close to the living accommodation as possible in a well lit area .&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>The gangway life buoy at manifold must NOT have the line attached to it.<o:p></o:p></span><u1:p></u1:p></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">On chemical tankers people who have no legitimate business must be refused access. The reason is ships security and well as distraction to limited crew on board who are all doing mandatory critical duties.&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>Master must liaise with agent and terminal to achieve this. The gangway watch must inform OOW if any of the authorized shore persons appear to be inebriated.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TR9vY4eyuVI/AAAAAAAACic/mQpVjdaY3lE/s1600/chm.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TR9vY4eyuVI/AAAAAAAACic/mQpVjdaY3lE/s1600/chm.jpg\" /></a></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: x-small;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 14px;\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )</span></span></div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "5", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/3342868703730720769/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "825317950093529852", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2011-01-01T21:27:00+05:30", "updated": "2018-10-08T13:48:58+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNTM4OTg2NzM4MzU1Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/01/isaac-newton-calculus-thief-capt-ajit.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/825317950093529852", "title": "ISAAC NEWTON , THE CALCULUS THIEF --  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TR9Lt4wQkyI/AAAAAAAAChk/ZrXdlueGk7c/s1600/image.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: large;\">ISAAC NEWTON- PATENTER OF STOLEN KNOWLEDGE</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: large;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-gJVkD1Wk6ZY/VBYq_vhKrlI/AAAAAAAAv5M/Tl6TxGzaD1k/s1600/tdte.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-gJVkD1Wk6ZY/VBYq_vhKrlI/AAAAAAAAv5M/Tl6TxGzaD1k/s1600/tdte.jpg\" width=\"336\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The whole world is under the impression that Isaac Newton is the father of Calculus.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\"><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The truth is that Calculus was understood and practised in Malabar of India which had the School of Astronomy and Mathematics , even before Christ was born. &nbsp;It was used to express Vedic physical laws in mathematical terms, and to calculate rates of change in Astronomy and Astrology.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-8vbttRs6sqM/TW5F_kLuqsI/AAAAAAAAD2Y/RnOy97OCsxg/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-8vbttRs6sqM/TW5F_kLuqsI/AAAAAAAAD2Y/RnOy97OCsxg/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\"><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Calicut my hometown was the Capital of Malabar, where Vasco da Gama landed in 1498. &nbsp;St Thomas ( disciple of Jesus ) had died in Malabar.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\"><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The great Pyramids of Egypt was designed by architects proficient in Astronomy and Vaastu from Calicut, with tunnels from the Pharaoh's chamber at 90 degrees between Alnilam of Orion belt and the North star..</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\"><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Aryabhatta born in Kerala ( my home state ) in 2700 BC, was one of the early members of this school. &nbsp;<span style=\"color: black;\">Aryabhatta was the first to calculate Pi of 3.1416 and the solar year of 365.358 days . He propounded a heliocentric universe 4200 years before Copernicus, with elliptically orbiting planets and a spherical earth spinning on its axis explaining the motion of the heavens. He was the father of plane / spherical Trigonometry and Algebra, when Europe was in the dark ages.. Today you don't see this pioneers name in the list of top 100 mathematicians.</span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Aryabhatta was the first to compute the circumference of the earth, with an error of just 64 miles.. Aryabhatta gave a method to find the cube root of numbers and dealt with arithmetic,geometric and indeterminate equations in algebra. He dealt with square, cube, triangle, trapezium, circle and sphere in geometry. font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">QUOTE: Al-Biruni wrote an encyclopedic work on India called \u201cTarikh Al-Hind\u201d (History of India) in which he explored nearly every aspect of Indian life, including religion, history, geography, geology, science, and mathematics. My book is nothing but a simple historic record of facts. I shall place before the reader the theories of the Hindus exactly as they are, and I shall mention in connection with them similar theories of the Greeks in order to show the relationship existing between them.(1910, Vol. 1, p. 7;1958, p. 5)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">Hindus considered Muslims violent and impure, and did not want to share anything with him.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">Over time, Al-Biruni won the welcome of Hindu scholars. Al-Biruni collected books and studied with these Hindu scholars to become fluent in Sanskrit, discover and translate into Arabic the mathematics, science, medicine, astronomy and other fields of arts as practiced in 11th century India. He was inspired by the arguments offered by Indian scholars who believed earth must be ellipsoid shape, with yet to be discovered continent at earth's south pole, and earth's rotation around the sun is the only way to fully explain the difference in daylight hours by latitude, seasons and earth's relative positions with moon and stars.[36] Al-Biruni was also critical of Indian scribes who he believed carelessly corrupted Indian documents while making copies of older documents.[37] Al-Biruni's translations as well as his own original contributions reached Europe in 12th and 13th century, where they were actively sought.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">CONTINUED TO 2--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">CONTINUED FROM 1--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">While others were killing each other over religious differences, Al-Biruni had a remarkable ability to engage Hindus in peaceful dialogue. Mohammad Yasin puts this dramatically when he says, \u201cThe Indica is like a magic island of quiet, impartial research in the midst of a world of clashing swords, burning towns, and burned temples.\u201d (Indica is another name for Al-Biruni\u2019s history of India). Al-Khw\u0101rizm\u012b accomplished most of his work in the period between 813 and 833. After the Muslim conquest of Persia, Baghdad became the centre of scientific studies and trade, and many merchants and scientists from as far as China and India traveled to this city, as did al-Khw\u0101rizm\u012b. He worked in Baghdad as a scholar at the House of Wisdom established by Caliph al-Ma\u2019m\u016bn, where he studied the sciences and mathematics, which included the translation of Greek and Sanskrit scientific manuscripts.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 18.4px;\">Al-Khw\u0101rizm\u012b's Z\u012bj al-Sindhind[11] (Arabic: \u0632\u064a\u062c \u0627\u0644\u0633\u0646\u062f \u0647\u0646\u062f\u200e, \"astronomical tables of Sindh and Hind\") is a work consisting of approximately 37 chapters on calendrical and astronomical calculations and 116 tables with calendrical, astronomical and astrological data, as well as a table of sine values. This is the first of many Arabic Zijes based on the Indian astronomical methods known as the sindhind.[22] The work contains tables for the movements of the sun, the moon and the five planets known at the time. This work marked the turning point in Islamic astronomy. Hitherto, Muslim astronomers had adopted a primarily research approach to the field, translating works of others and learning already discovered knowledge.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-size: 16px; margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_175M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888;\">Capt. Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2017/12/blockchain-bitcoin-big-brother-will.html?showComment=1513185259860#c4671100578196233665\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888;\">December 13, 2017 at 10:44 PM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_175MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nPhysicists in China and the US have built a 10-qubit superconducting quantum processor that could be scaled up to tackle problems not solvable by classical computers.<br />\n<br />\nQubits are the building blocks of quantum computing, capable of superposition \u2013 being in two states at the same time, rather than the computer bits of today, which are either a 1 or a 0 at any given moment.<br />\n<br />\nEntanglement is where quantum states can't be described independently, but only in relation to the others, making for a more solid system. The team used a measurement technique called quantum tomography to prove that they had indeed entangled their qubits<br />\n<br />\nThe phenomenon of entanglement in quantum physics, which has been observed in many experiments, implies that objects that are far removed in space (even across billions of miles) remain connected even though there is no mediating agency.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/01/quantum-entanglement-video-capt-ajit.html</span><br />\n<br />\nVedic philosophy tells us about the existence of another type of particle called the atma, the soul, the self, having different properties from those of ordinary particles.This is not unusual in physics, as is the case with antimatter particles.<br />\n<br />\nThe atma does not come into or out of existence, it is always present. It does not decay or degrade, it maintains its individuality always, it\u2019s infinitesimally small and it\u2019s not composed of more elementary particles. It\u2019s unchangeable, which along with the individuality property implies that it does not unite with other particles to create more complex structures, nor does it merge with others.<br />\n<br />\nThe atma does not interact directly with matter, but given that the atma is the source of consciousness and the life force in a living entity, any entity displaying them reveals the presence of an atma in it\u2014whether human, animal, plant, etc.<br />\n<br />\nVedanta wrote 7000 years ago-- The living entities are not made up of atmas; rather, they are these particles and are animating the material bodies that encase them. As soon as the atma leaves one body for another, the old body no longer exhibits consciousness or life symptoms, and begins to degrade.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/02/daltons-atomic-theory-sage-kashyapa-and.html</span><br />\n<br />\nMaharishi Kashyapa is also known as Kanada Muni.
