V.S 1.1.6<br />\nThe forces to be considered are an external force, gravity, that with causes attraction of particles, that which causes repulsion of particles and the internal movements of them in matter.<br />\n<br />\nV.S 1.1.13 Action is opposed by an equivalent opposite reaction<br />\nV.S 5.1.1618 The diversities of the movement of an arrow are due to the consecutive changes in the components of the acting forces. The stored energy provides the propulsion to the arrow and this causes it move further to a high point. This component keeps reducing while that of gravity increases resulting in its fall.Once the work against gravity ceases then the body reaches an energyless state falling under gravity.<br />\nV.S 1.1.27 The force on a body is the resultant of gravity and the work done against it.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nCONTINUED TO 2-</div>\n</div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; Also, this change is in the direction of the force. Suppose that the mass of an object is \u2018m\u2019 and in time interval \u2018t\u2019, the velocity of the object changes from \u2018u\u2019 to \u2018v\u2019 due to the force acting on it.<br />\n<br />\nThen, Initial momentum = m*u<br />\nFinal momentum = m*v<br />\nChange in momentum = m(v*u)<br />\nTherefore, the rate of change of momentum = m(v*u)/t<br />\nt = m*a (from Kanada\u2019s first law)<br />\n<br />\nFrom Kandas second law, force is proportional to the rate of change of momentum<br />\nOr, p = k*m*a (where k is a constant)<br />\nIf m=1 and a=1, then<br />\n1 = k*1*1 or k = 1<br />\nOr, p = m*a<br />\n<br />\nTherefore, unit force is the one that produces unit acceleration in an object of unit mass. Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2018/03/fatawa-e-alamgiri-kosher-document-of_13.html?showComment=1521004208510#c7672584269921191275\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">March 14, 2018 at 10:40 AM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_28MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nCONTINUED FROM 1--<br />\n<br />\nAnd it's important to know the Sun's position, because it's used for normal time-keeping (solar time, rather than sidereal time). By Kepler's Second Law, the Earth orbits faster at perihelion and slower at aphelion. ..<br />\n<br />\nSo the Sun appears to move fastest along ecliptic in January and slowest in July. ..<br />\n<br />\nWe can invent an imaginary Sun (the dynamical mean Sun) which coincides with the true Sun when the Earth is at perihelion, but moves along the ecliptic at a constant speed. ..<br />\n<br />\nThe true Sun appears to move faster than the dynamical mean Sun when the Earth is around perihelion, and slower when the Earth is near aphelion: one cycle per year. However, an object moving at a constant speed along the ecliptic is still moving at a varying speed with respect to the equator, since the ecliptic is tilted to the equator. ..<br />\n<br />\nWe invent another imaginary Sun, called simply the mean Sun, which moves along the equator at constant speed; the dynamical mean Sun appears to lag behind this where the ecliptic is steeply tilted to the equator (around the equinoxes) and catch up where it's nearly parallel (around the solstices): two cycles per year\u2026<br />\n<br />\nCombining these two effects gives the total difference in time between the true Sun and the mean Sun, which is called the equation of time.. The true Sun is about 14 minutes late, compared to the mean Sun, around 10th February, about 4 minutes early around May 15th, about 6 minutes late around July 25th, and about 16 minutes early around November 5th\u2026<br />\n<br />\nThe interval between two meridian transits of the mean Sun is the mean solar day. ..<br />\n<br />\nThe upper transit of the mean Sun across the local meridian marks midday, local mean time. Greenwich Mean Time (GMT) is defined as midday when the mean Sun crosses the meridian of Greenwich..<br />\n<br />\nApparent solar time, as measured by the the true Sun (e.g. on a sundial), may differ from GMT for three reasons. ..<br />\n<br />\nFirstly, because of the equation of time, Secondly, because of the longitude of the observer (the further west, the later the Sun will cross the meridian)\u2026.Thirdly, because of \"Summer Time\"\u2026<br />\n<br />\nBritain uses GMT as standard time in winter, adding one hour in summer. Most other countries adopt their own standard time, suitable for their own longitude (large countries may have several time-zones), differing from GMT by a set amount. In practice, the Earth's rotation is not quite constant. ..<br />\n<br />\nTime is now regulated by atomic clocks, and called Coordinated Universal Time (UTC), but this is artificially kept within 1 second of GMT by adding a \"leap second\" when necessary..<br />\n<br />\nKERALA ASTROMOMERS KNEW THIS WHEN THE WHITE MAN WAS USING GRUNT GRUNT FOR LANGUAGE ..<br />\n<br />\ncapt ajit vadakayil<br />\n..</div>\n</div>\n</li>\n</span></ol>\n<span id=\"bc_0_29b+seedIY6D\" kind=\"d\">\n</span></div>\n<span id=\"bc_0_29b+seedIY6D\" kind=\"d\">\n</span></div>\n</div>\n</li>\n</span></ol>\n<span id=\"bc_0_74b+seed9f-D\" kind=\"d\">\n</span></div>\n<span id=\"bc_0_74b+seed9f-D\" kind=\"d\">\n</span></div>\n</li>\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"bc_0_18B\" kind=\"b\" style=\"background-color: #eeeeee; border-bottom: 0px; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0.25em 0px 0px;\"><div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; float: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n<img src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-0Gvy5mBcipE/WlAJZNfU3zI/AAAAAAABXsU/wZaBJr4cOoclmnshY0dz6Y3NbokDpLaaACK4BGAYYCw/s35/*\" style=\"border: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); max-width: 36px;\" /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c56934804452688012\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_34M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. herbs\u2026</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nThere are five concepts of the substance, namely:--</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nrasa (taste),</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\ngu\u1e47a (properties),</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nv\u012brya (potency),</div>\n<div style=\"font-size: 16px;\">\nvip\u0101ka (rasa , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"color: black; But when Hitler annexed the German speaking Austria , the Japs annexed Chinese Manchuria and the Italians annexed Ethiopia, his gargantuan belly rumbled!&nbsp; How sensitive!<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">He would take his first whisky and soda soon after breakfast. For the rest of the day the tumbler was never empty . He used to be drunk throughout the day.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; He always had a glass of whisky by him, and he drank brandy and champagne both at lunchtime and dinner.&nbsp; He never missed having a bottle of champagne for lunch and very often had another one for dinner.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">His aide had written &nbsp;\u201c After his regular afternoon nap he would have two or three glasses of iced whisky and soda before dinner, at which he always had champagne, followed by several doses of brandy ; this would be followed by several whisky and sodas as the night wore on\u201d</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When Churchill travelled to the US during Prohibition, he obtained a doctor's note to certify that regular consumption of alcoholic spirits was necessary to his health. Churchill's heavy drinking pissed off President Roosevelt who complained that Sir Winston was drunk all the time.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">He is on record as having once drunk 11 of these during a single meal and then boasting about it. &nbsp;He insisted than Europeans loved leaders who could hold their liquor.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">On the 2 April, 1940 he was too drunk to finish a speech in the Commons and had to be led away.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 24px;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">He was known to be a manic depressive. He was prescribed Laudanum for his bipolar disorder-- to prevent him going off on tangent, during the war .</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In 2006, a British mental health charity defended a statue it commissioned of Churchill in a straitjacket, after the statue sparked an outcry. font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><i>The Supreme Authority\nof the Holy Office, in a decree dated 15 November 1957, forbade the works of de\nChardin to be retained in libraries, including those of religious institutes.\nHis books were not to be sold in Catholic bookshops and were not to be\ntranslated in other languages.<o:p></o:p></i></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><i>A decree of the Holy\nOffice dated 30 June 1963, under the authority of Pope John XXIII warned that\n\u201c. . . it is obvious that in philosophical and theological matters, the said\nworks (de Chardin\u2019s) are replete with ambiguities or rather with serious errors\nwhich offend Catholic doctrine.<o:p></o:p></i></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><i>The Vicariate of Rome\n(a diocese ruled in the name of Pope Paul VI by his Cardinal Vicar) in a decree\ndated 30 September 1963 , required that Catholic booksellers in Rome should\nwithdraw from circulation the works of de Chardin, together with those books\nwhich favour his erroneous doctrines.</i></span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRrQrJEI6MI/AAAAAAAACc0/4oRU3ar8z2M/s1600/dark.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "65", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/4896973456816126950/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "6912438986694991075", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-12-29T08:29:00+05:30", "updated": "2012-07-27T09:25:24+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzQzMzYxMzI0MDg0Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/12/static-electricity-on-chemical-tankers.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/6912438986694991075", "title": "STATIC ELECTRICITY ON CHEMICAL TANKERS --  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">A few years ago , a chemical tanker exploded with loss of most hands.&nbsp;</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">There the crew had attempted to \"fast forward dry\" &nbsp;the sump of a cargo tank containing MTBE by blowing air via the Framo suction , rather than doing a bottom flush with water.&nbsp;</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">MTBE is a static accumulator.</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i style=\"color: blue;\">This real reason is buried--as </i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; color: red;\">AFTER AN ACCIDENT AT SEA , TRUTH IS ALWAYS THE FIRST CASUALITY.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv38LVKWZI/AAAAAAAACdg/ML3OeD2bAR8/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv38LVKWZI/AAAAAAAACdg/ML3OeD2bAR8/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\"></span>People involved have to protect their backsides, company has to collect insurance and laugh all the way to the bank , ignorant souls in the safety dept have to write beautiful post mortems and personally shine, Vetting houses have to be fooled . &nbsp;Hardly anybody cares for the poor dead sailors or their families.</span></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Static electricity</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"> is generated by friction which happens during relative motion. Electrostatic charges can accumulate in poor conductors or insulated good conductors. If two such bodies with accumulated static electricity are brought close together, a spark jumps between the bodies. Almost everybody has experienced such crackling discharge when removing a nylon shirt from a warm body in a&nbsp; cold dry cabin. If this spark is incendive it could ignite a flammble atmosphere. Such discharge must be prevented, unless the atmosphere is inert.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4AUQtOpI/AAAAAAAACdk/xvxHuawfLUo/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4AUQtOpI/AAAAAAAACdk/xvxHuawfLUo/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Static electricity can happen due to-&nbsp; Charge separation (turbulent flow of a static accumulator liquid) ,&nbsp; Charge accumulation (introduction of a non bonded object like a sampler) , Electrostatic discharge (the non bonded object with accumulated charge comes close to an earth and an spark will occur. such spark is incendive ),&nbsp; Electrostatic discharges with sufficient energy can ignite flammable hydrocarbon gas/air mixtures.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">All three of these stages are necessary for an electrostatic ignition.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<a href=\"http://www.blogger.com/post-edit.g?blogID=3564735312144269387&amp;postID=6912438986694991075\" name=\"Charge_Separation\"></a><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Whenever two dissimilar materials come into contact <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">charge separation</i></b> occurs at the interface. The interface may be between a solid and a liquid or between two immiscible liquids. &nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Examples:&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The flow of liquids (e.g. through pipes or fine filters,&nbsp; the settling of an immiscible liquid through a liquid (e.g.&nbsp; water through&nbsp;kerosene),&nbsp; the ejection of steam from a nozzle , the splashing or agitation of a liquid against a solid surface (e.g. water washing operations or the&nbsp;initial turbulence involved in filling a tank with oil), the vigorous rubbing together of certain synthetic polymers (e.g. the sliding of a polypropylene rope through PVC gloved hands). <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When the charges are separated, a large potential difference develops between them. Also a voltage distribution is set up throughout the neighbouring space and this is known as an&nbsp; electrostatic field .If an uncharged conductor is present in an electrostatic field it picks up the same voltage as the field it occupies. Charge one end of the conductor gives an equal and opposite charge at the other end. This is capable of contributing to an electrostatic charge. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<a href=\"http://www.blogger.com/post-edit.g?blogID=3564735312144269387&amp;postID=6912438986694991075\" name=\"Charge_Accumulation\"></a><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Charges which have been separated attempt to recombine and to neutralise each other. This process is known as charge relaxation. If one, or both, of the separated materials carrying charge is an insulator recombination is impeded and the material <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">&nbsp;accumulates the charge</i></b> upon it. The period of time for which the charge is retained is characterised by the relaxation time of the material, which is related to its conductivity; the lower the conductivity the greater is the relaxation time.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4F-w2v7I/AAAAAAAACdo/szXeUP57658/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4F-w2v7I/AAAAAAAACdo/szXeUP57658/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If a material has a comparatively high conductivity, the recombination of charges is very rapid and no static electricity accumulates on the material. Such a highly conducting material can only retain or accumulate charge if it is insulated and the rate of loss of charge is then dependent upon the relaxation time of this insulator.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<a href=\"http://www.blogger.com/post-edit.g?blogID=3564735312144269387&amp;postID=6912438986694991075\" name=\"Electrostatic_Discharges\"></a><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Electrostatic discharge</span></i></b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">, is dependent upon the strength of the electrostatic field in the space between the points. This field strength, or voltage gradient, is given approximately by dividing the difference in voltage between the points by their distance apart. A field strength of about 3,000 kilovolts per metre is sufficient to cause breakdown of air or petroleum gases. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4LaQRDeI/AAAAAAAACds/ef8twjnf8R4/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4LaQRDeI/AAAAAAAACds/ef8twjnf8R4/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The field strength near protrusions is greater than the overall field strength in the vicinity and discharges therefore generally occur at protrusions. A discharge may occur between a protrusion and the space in its vicinity without reaching another object. These single electrode discharges are not incendive in the context of normal tanker operations.&nbsp;The alternative is a discharge between two electrodes adjacent to each other.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4PyxloII/AAAAAAAACdw/kpK-Hs_H7ds/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4PyxloII/AAAAAAAACdw/kpK-Hs_H7ds/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Examples are:&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Between sampling apparatus lowered into a tank and the surface of a charged petroleum liquid.&nbsp;&nbsp;Between an unearthed object floating on the surface of a charged liquid and the adjacent tank&nbsp; structure.&nbsp; &nbsp;Between unearthed equipment suspended in a tank and the adjacent tank structure&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">All&nbsp; liquids the whole range of aqueous solutions including sea water are conductors. The human body, consisting of about 60% water, is effectively a liquid conductor. The important property of conductors is that they incapable of holding a charge unless insulated. But if they are insulated and an opportunity for an electrical discharge occurs all the charge available is&nbsp; instantaneously released .&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Sparks between two conductors are more potent than the ones between objects, one of which is not a conductor. In the latter case, discharges often take a more diffuse and much less dangerous form, known as corona or brush discharge, rather than a spark.&nbsp; Corona or st Elmo\u2019s fire does not have sufficient energy to start an explosion ( ion emission of blue colour ).&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4UvMdNgI/AAAAAAAACd0/0lv9BXi3Trs/s1600/download.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4UvMdNgI/AAAAAAAACd0/0lv9BXi3Trs/s1600/download.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Spark energy may be reduced by physical factors such as electrode resistance, spark gap distance, and large gap areas. Discharges are sometimes in the form of a \"corona\", an ionization of gas which is not incendive but may precede an incendive spark.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The second group is the insulators who retain a received charge for a very long period.&nbsp; Charged non-conductors cause concern because they can transfer charge to, or induce charge on, neighbouring insulated conductors which may then give rise to sparks. Very highly charged non-conductors may themselves contribute directly to incendive sparks.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Gases are good insulators. Charged mists are formed during the ejection of wet steam. Though water, has high conductivity, the relaxation of the charge on the droplets is retarded by the insulating properties of the surrounding gas. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Electrostatic discharges can occur when a static accumulator oil (such as toluene) pumped turbulently into a tank.,electrically isolated liquid or solid conductors, for example mists in air, or a metal rod hanging on the end of a synthetic fibre rope.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRwgMDuVzjI/AAAAAAAACec/wXAEK84br2g/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRwgMDuVzjI/AAAAAAAACec/wXAEK84br2g/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<a href=\"http://www.blogger.com/post-edit.g?blogID=3564735312144269387&amp;postID=6912438986694991075\" name=\"General_Precautions\"></a><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The most important countermeasure that must be taken to prevent an electrostatic hazard is to bond all metal objects together. Bonding eliminates the risk of discharges between metal objects, which can be incendive. To avoid discharges from conductors to earth, it is normal practice to earth ( grounding). On ships, bonding to earth is effectively accomplished by connecting metallic objects to the metal structure of the ship, which is naturally earthed through the sea. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Some examples of objects which might be electrically insulated in hazardous situations and which must therefore be bonded are:&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Ship/shore hose flanges if more than one length of non-conducting hose is used . Portable tank cleaning machines.&nbsp; Conducting manual ullaging and sampling equipment. The probe of an UTI tape .&nbsp; Floating cans must not be inadvertently be left inside cargo tanks. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Charge generation is enhanced ----if water droplets are suspended in the oil as it flows through the pipes, or flow through a&nbsp; filter of the kind used for aircraft jet fuels. These filters have the ability&nbsp; to charge fuels to a very high level, probably because all the fuel is brought into intimate contact with the filter surface, where charge separation occurs or by turbulence and splashing in the early stages of pumping say toluene into an empty tank or the settling of water droplets stirred up by a static accumulator oil in the tank. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Fine particles during discharge of pressurised liquid carbon dioxide are&nbsp; charged .During the discharge of pressurised liquid carbon dioxide, the rapid cooling which takes place can result in the formation of particles of solid carbon dioxide which become charged on impact&nbsp; with the nozzle and can thereby lead to incendive sparks. Carbon dioxide should therefore not be injected into cargo tanks or pump rooms which may contain unignited flammable gas mixtures. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Only conductors are able to release sufficient energy to ignite an explosive vapor.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When the field strength around a charged body reaches a certain value, different kinds of discharge may occur. To start a fire or explosion such a discharge must possess sufficient energy. It has been shown that a spark between 2 electrodes has to possess an amount of energy of about 0.2mj to ignite an explosive propane mixture. For ammonia the necessary amount is &gt; by 600 times.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Liquids are considered to be static accumulators if have conductivities less than 50 picoSiemens/metre (pS/m) giving relaxation times greater than 0.35 seconds. A static accumulator may carry sufficient charge to constitute an incendive ingnition hazard during loading into the tank, and for upto 30 min after completion of loading. Examples: Clean oils (distillates). An antistatic additive is a substance which is deliberately added to a petroleum distillate to raise its conductivity.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Antistatic additives raises the electrical conductivity &gt;100 pico siemens/ metre.&nbsp; Antistatic precautions are not necessary in an inerted tank. The effectiveness of the antistatic additives&nbsp; is dependent upon the length of time since the additive was introduced into the product, the ambient temperature , and satisfactory product mixing.&nbsp; It can never be certain that a products conductivity is above 100 pS/m unless it is continuously measured.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The generation of static electricity cannot be prevented absolutely, because its intrinsic origins are present at every interface. The conductivity of a liquid determines whether or not it retains the generated static charge. Loading rate precautions are not necessary for gasolines and some aviation fuels because of their low viscosity and low friction. \"Avjet JP 4\" and middle distillates require loading precautions to prevent static accumulation<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Known static accumulators are\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Cumene<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Cyclohexane<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Diethyl ether<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Heptane<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Jet fuels<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Kerosene<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">MTBE<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Nonene<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Octane<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Styrene<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Toluene<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Xylene<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Gasolene&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Electrostatic generation is restricted in the initial stages of loading by reducing the loading rate until all turbulence in the tank has ceased.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">At the commencement of loading an empty tank the linear velocity in the branch line to each individual cargo tank should not exceed 1 metre/second.&nbsp; Mixtures of oil and water constitute a most potent source of static&nbsp;electricity. When an accumulator cargo moves through a pipeline it leaves a charge on the metal and picks an opposite charge. It also picks up a charge due to turbulence when it first enters a tank.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">By reducing the initial and max loading rates\u2014the accumulated static charge is kept too low to cause an incendiary spark. Inerted tanks do not need the 30 minute moratorium.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Fixed washing machines or high level alarms, may act as isolated probes. A metal probe remote from any other tank structure but near a highly charged liquid surface will have a high voltage gradient at the probe tip. During the loading of static accumulator oils, this high voltage gradient may cause electrostatic discharges to the approaching liquid surface.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">A person who is highly insulated from earth by his footwear or the surface on which he is standing can become electrostatically charged. Electrostatic discharges caused by clothing and footwear do not present a significant hazard at high humidities. However boiler suits should not be made of synthetic materials. </span><br />\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Metallic components of any equipment to be lowered into a tank should be securely bonded together and earthed to the ship before introduction and should remain earthed until after removal. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4fYS42VI/AAAAAAAACd4/R0yzGysMWW8/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4fYS42VI/AAAAAAAACd4/R0yzGysMWW8/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">A significant electrostatic charge can be generated when a polypropylene rope runs rapidly through a PVC-gloved hand. For this reason only natural fibre ropes should be used for dipping, ullaging and sampling. </span><br />\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Lightning may strike ship if an ionized path is created by gas flow to the atmosphere. So it is better to stop loading/gas freeing in still air conditions, to prevent gas accumulation on deck, when lightning threatens. A distant thunderstorm may produce heavy charges on board. Wind speed of &gt; 5m/ sec is required to disperse gases.</span><br />\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-XBMbWcvgh0o/UBIRG5mqcgI/AAAAAAAAOIE/hoyYpziJMzE/s1600/sdgjk.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"212\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-XBMbWcvgh0o/UBIRG5mqcgI/AAAAAAAAOIE/hoyYpziJMzE/s320/sdgjk.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Static accumulator cargoes should not be handled at flow rates &gt; 7ms/ s when loading kerosene, toluene start at slow speed &lt;1 m/ sec in pipes. Until the turbulence at the tank bottom has ceased.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRwgEUzozRI/AAAAAAAACeY/4KanXSnRZ6s/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRwgEUzozRI/AAAAAAAACeY/4KanXSnRZ6s/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Insulating flange at shore connection is better than bonding wire via a flame proof switch ( to prevent ship and jetty to form a voltaic cell as the hoses have bonding wire.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Ship to shore bonding is not effective as a safety device and may even be dangerous. If local regulations require the use of a bonding cable, then the Chief Officer must ensure that it is connected before the first hose is put aboard and not disconnected until after the last hose has been removed. The connection must be at the shipside, well clear of the manifold area.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When a ship-shore bonding cable is used, it must be used in the following manner:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When connecting:<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">-open switch<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">-connect bonding cable to ship away from any possible source of ignition such as drip trays<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">-close switch<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">-connect hose.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When disconnecting:<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">-disconnect hose<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">-open switch<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">-remove bonding cable.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Only if the jetty is without an insulating flange and is devoid of impressed current protection, should consideration be given to switching off the ship's system.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The ship's system should only be switched off as provided for by the above, or if required by terminal regulations. In view of the possibility of an incendiary spark above the water line, on the ship's initial contact with a jetty or other ship, it is necessary to curtail all activities, which would provide a source of hydrocarbon vapour during the berthing process.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If in any doubt as to whether a particular cargo is a static accumulator or not it should be treated as such a product and the precautions described followed. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRwf-P5gyaI/AAAAAAAACeU/XHUlPPgvz-o/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRwf-P5gyaI/AAAAAAAACeU/XHUlPPgvz-o/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">It must be ensured that the MF/HF SSB (GMDSS) is earthed at the berth during cargo operations..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Before cleaning a tank containing a static accumulator like toluene the bottom should be flushed with water and stripped. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If portable cleaning machines are used all hoses and hose connections should be tested for electrical continuity. Connections should not be removed unless the machine has been removed from the tank.. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The tank should be kept drained during washing.&nbsp;Ropes of synthetic fibres should not be used to support the tank cleaning machines. The UTI MMC tapes used must be earthed. UTI tube is slotted so as not to allow any significant electrical charge to accumulate on the surface of liquid within the sounding pipe. UTI tapes which have quick couplings to connect to vapour lock do not need bonding wires\u2014the internal bonding of such unit should be checked every 6 months in accordance to man instrns.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRwf6WFf_RI/AAAAAAAACeQ/4_QVwUE9kNk/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRwf6WFf_RI/AAAAAAAACeQ/4_QVwUE9kNk/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Avoid recirculation in a non gasfree tank. Steam&nbsp; must never be injected, if tank is not gas free. No machine may have greater throughput than 60m3/h and no nozzle may have greater throughput than 17.5 m3/h. The total water throughput per cargo tank must not exceed 110 m3/hr.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Water washing, causes electrostatically charged mist. The electrostatic levels vary widely from tank to tank, both in magnitude and in sign.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When washing is started in a dirty tank the charge in the mist is initially negative, reaches a maximum negative value, then goes back through zero and finally rises towards a positive equilibrium value. The level and polarity of charge depends on the wash water and the degree of cleanliness of the tank. Recirculation of tank cleaning chemicals,&nbsp; may cause very high electrostatic potentials in the mist. Potentials are higher in large tanks than in small ones. The size and number of washing machines in a tank affect the rate of change of charge. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Steaming can produce electrostatically charged clouds. Steam can cause very much higher levels of charging at a lesser time than those produced by water washing. Steam should not be injected into cargo tanks where there is a flammable atmosphere.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Experiments have shown that high capacity, single nozzle fixed washing machines can produce water slugs which, owing to their size, trajectory and duration before breaking up, may satisfy the criteria for producing incendive discharges. On the other hand, there is no evidence of such water slugs being produced by portable types of washing machine. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Unearthed conducting objects must not be introduced in a tank when there is charged mist. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Tankcleaning hoses must be tested for electrical continuity. Max 6 ohms/ meter length.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The plastic or polyethylene sleeves used for gas freeing can accumulate charge.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRwf12HokxI/AAAAAAAACeM/6FwXMBu3e-Q/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRwf12HokxI/AAAAAAAACeM/6FwXMBu3e-Q/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If air or inert gas is blown into the bottom of a tank containing a static accumulator oil a strong electrostatic field can be generated, especially in the presence of water or particulate matter. So it may not be a wise idea to blow through the sump to dry it out . It is better to bottom flush and strip. Inert gas too blown into the bottom of a tank can generate a strong electrostatic charge by bubbling action and agitation of the fluid.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">An isolated probe configuration can be avoided by installing the device adjacent to a wall or other tank structure to reduce the voltage gradient at the probe tip. Alternatively, a support can be added running from the lower end to the tank structure so that the rising liquid meets an edge rather than the isolated tip of a probe. Or the protrusion could be earthed by a wire as is usually done on chemical tankers. <i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">The best</i> <i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">solution is to construct the probe-like device entirely of a <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">non-conductive material</b></i>. These measures are not necessary if the vessel is limited to crude, black oil service where the tanks are inerted. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">It is not a right practice to allow&nbsp; violent wave motion in static accumulator tanks due to free surface.. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">A person who is highly insulated from earth by his footwear or the surface on which he is standing can become electrostatically charged. Electrostatic discharges caused by clothing and footwear do not present a significant hazard at high humidities. However boiler suits should not be made of synthetic materials. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4n4Qk3WI/AAAAAAAACd8/Q6Ob4Ke6NG8/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4n4Qk3WI/AAAAAAAACd8/Q6Ob4Ke6NG8/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Metallic components of any equipment to be lowered into a tank should be securely bonded together and earthed to the ship before introduction and should remain earthed until after removal. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">A significant electrostatic charge can be generated when a polypropylene rope runs rapidly through a PVC-gloved hand. For this reason only natural fibre ropes should be used for dipping, ullaging and sampling. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRwfvhx1-RI/AAAAAAAACeI/By-Iis53q6E/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRwfvhx1-RI/AAAAAAAACeI/By-Iis53q6E/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Lightning may strike ship if an ionized path is created by gas flow to the atmosphere.so better to stop loading and gas freeing especially in still air conditions, to prevent gas accumulation on deck. A distant thunderstorm may produce heavy charges on board. Streamers from lightning rods can ignite\u2014relates in tanks as sparks coming from protruding objects towards a charged mist.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv40UvrAhI/AAAAAAAACeE/You59LwHvSc/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv40UvrAhI/AAAAAAAACeE/You59LwHvSc/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4sYPY9II/AAAAAAAACeA/RbHwoVuS2Uc/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRv4sYPY9II/AAAAAAAACeA/RbHwoVuS2Uc/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">IBC code requires that all gasketed cargo pipes, joints and hose connections&nbsp; to be electrically bonded.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Air driven lamps must have water traps for the air supply. The supply hose should be of low electrical resistance.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">All bonding arrangements on board must be regularly inspected with records of the inspections maintained. When maintenance work is carried out on the cargo system, checks must be made to ensure that the bonding&nbsp;&nbsp; arrangements have been reinstated correctly.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">It is our policy NOT to allow Toluene spraying due to danger of static explosion.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRqguWReuUI/AAAAAAAACcY/AFGVgxmJ8Ho/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRqguWReuUI/AAAAAAAACcY/AFGVgxmJ8Ho/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><o:p>&nbsp;CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div>\n</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "24", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/6912438986694991075/comments"}}], "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/MjAxOS0wNC0yMlQxMTozNzoyOS43MjRa\""}
